Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core

                            is guess

-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core

Option     Filename  Type         Description
------------------------------------------------------------
  -s NVT_sam33_water8000_next.tpr  Input        Run input file: tpr tpb tpa
  -o NVT_sam33_water8000.trr  Output       Full precision trajectory: trr trj
                                   cpt
  -x NVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Output, Opt. Compressed trajectory (portable
                                   xdr format)
-cpi NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Input, Opt!  Checkpoint file
-cpo NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Output, Opt. Checkpoint file
  -c NVT_sam33_water8000.gro  Output       Structure file: gro g96 pdb etc.
  -e NVT_sam33_water8000.edr  Output       Energy file
  -g NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output       Log file
-dhdlNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-fieldVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tableVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tabletf_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablepT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablebT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-rerunVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Input, Opt.  Trajectory: xtc trr trj gro g96
                                   pdb cpt
-tpi NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tpidNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ei NVT_sam33_water8000.edi  Input, Opt.  ED sampling input
 -eo NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
  -j NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Input, Opt.  General coupling stuff
 -jo NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Output, Opt. General coupling stuff
-ffoutVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-devoutT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-runavVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -px NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -pf NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ro NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ra NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rs NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rt NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
-mtx NVT_sam33_water8000.mtx  Output, Opt. Hessian matrix
 -dn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Output, Opt. Index file
-multidirsam33_water8000  Input, Opt., Mult. Run directory
-membedT_sam33_water8000.dat  Input, Opt.  Generic data file
 -mp NVT_sam33_water8000.top  Input, Opt.  Topology file
 -mn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Input, Opt.  Index file

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id   Option     Filename  Type         Description

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

-mtx NVT_sam33_water8000.mtx  Output, Opt. Hessian matrix
 -dn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Output, Opt. Index file
-multidirsam33_water8000  Input, Opt., Mult. Run directory
-membedT_sam33_water8000.dat  Input, Opt.  Generic data file
 -mp NVT_sam33_water8000.top  Input, Opt.  Topology file
 -mn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Input, Opt.  Index file

                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
    Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

                            physical core

                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id   -pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id   -xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id   -deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none

-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize

                            is guess

                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

                            to start (0 is -ntomp)

                            auto, on or off

                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core

                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core

-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency

                            reproducibility

-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed

-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

------------------------------------------------------------
  -s NVT_sam33_water8000_next.tpr  Input        Run input file: tpr tpb tpa
  -o NVT_sam33_water8000.trr  Output       Full precision trajectory: trr trj
                                   cpt
  -x NVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Output, Opt. Compressed trajectory (portable
                                   xdr format)
-cpi NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Input, Opt!  Checkpoint file
-cpo NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Output, Opt. Checkpoint file
  -c NVT_sam33_water8000.gro  Output       Structure file: gro g96 pdb etc.
  -e NVT_sam33_water8000.edr  Output       Energy file
  -g NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output       Log file
-dhdlNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-fieldVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tableVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tabletf_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablepT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablebT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-rerunVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Input, Opt.  Trajectory: xtc trr trj gro g96
                                   pdb cpt
-tpi NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tpidNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ei NVT_sam33_water8000.edi  Input, Opt.  ED sampling input
 -eo NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
  -j NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Input, Opt.  General coupling stuff
 -jo NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Output, Opt. General coupling stuff
-ffoutVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-devoutT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-runavVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -px NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -pf NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ro NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ra NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rs NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rt NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
-mtx NVT_sam33_water8000.mtx  Output, Opt. Hessian matrix
 -dn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Output, Opt. Index file
-multidirsam33_water8000  Input, Opt., Mult. Run directory
-membedT_sam33_water8000.dat  Input, Opt.  Generic data file
 -mp NVT_sam33_water8000.top  Input, Opt.  Topology file
 -mn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Input, Opt.  Index file

-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme

                            reproducibility

-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files

                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names

                            option

                            period (steps)

                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.

Option     Filename  Type         Description
------------------------------------------------------------
  -s      topol.tpr  Input        Run input file: tpr tpb tpa
  -o       traj.trr  Output       Full precision trajectory: trr trj cpt
  -x       traj.xtc  Output, Opt. Compressed trajectory (portable xdr format)
-cpi      state.cpt  Input, Opt.  Checkpoint file
-cpo      state.cpt  Output, Opt. Checkpoint file
  -c    confout.gro  Output       Structure file: gro g96 pdb etc.
  -e       ener.edr  Output       Energy file
  -g         md.log  Output       Log file
-dhdl      dhdl.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-field    field.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-table    table.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tabletf    tabletf.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablep  tablep.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tableb   table.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-rerun    rerun.xtc  Input, Opt.  Trajectory: xtc trr trj gro g96 pdb cpt
-tpi        tpi.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tpid   tpidist.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ei        sam.edi  Input, Opt.  ED sampling input
 -eo      edsam.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
  -j       wham.gct  Input, Opt.  General coupling stuff
 -jo        bam.gct  Output, Opt. General coupling stuff
-ffout      gct.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-devout   deviatie.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-runav  runaver.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -px      pullx.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -pf      pullf.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ro   rotation.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ra  rotangles.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rs   rotslabs.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rt  rottorque.log  Output, Opt. Log file
-mtx         nm.mtx  Output, Opt. Hessian matrix
 -dn     dipole.ndx  Output, Opt. Index file
-multidir    rundir  Input, Opt., Mult. Run directory
-membed  membed.dat  Input, Opt.  Generic data file
 -mp     membed.top  Input, Opt.  Topology file
 -mn     membed.ndx  Input, Opt.  Index file

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string         Set the default filename for all file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   no      Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   no      Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   -1      Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

Option     Filename  Type         Description
------------------------------------------------------------
  -s NVT_sam33_water8000_next.tpr  Input        Run input file: tpr tpb tpa
  -o NVT_sam33_water8000.trr  Output       Full precision trajectory: trr trj
                                   cpt
  -x NVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Output, Opt. Compressed trajectory (portable
                                   xdr format)
-cpi NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Input, Opt!  Checkpoint file
-cpo NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Output, Opt. Checkpoint file
  -c NVT_sam33_water8000.gro  Output       Structure file: gro g96 pdb etc.
  -e NVT_sam33_water8000.edr  Output       Energy file
  -g NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output       Log file
-dhdlNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-fieldVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tableVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tabletf_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablepT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablebT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-rerunVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Input, Opt.  Trajectory: xtc trr trj gro g96
                                   pdb cpt
-tpi NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tpidNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ei NVT_sam33_water8000.edi  Input, Opt.  ED sampling input
 -eo NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
  -j NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Input, Opt.  General coupling stuff
 -jo NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Output, Opt. General coupling stuff
-ffoutVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-devoutT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-runavVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -px NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -pf NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ro NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ra NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rs NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rt NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
-mtx NVT_sam33_water8000.mtx  Output, Opt. Hessian matrix
 -dn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Output, Opt. Index file
-multidirsam33_water8000  Input, Opt., Mult. Run directory
-membedT_sam33_water8000.dat  Input, Opt.  Generic data file
 -mp NVT_sam33_water8000.top  Input, Opt.  Topology file
 -mn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Input, Opt.  Index file

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
Option     Filename  Type         Description
------------------------------------------------------------
  -s NVT_sam33_water8000_next.tpr  Input        Run input file: tpr tpb tpa
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
  -o NVT_sam33_water8000.trr  Output       Full precision trajectory: trr trj
                                   cpt
  -x NVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Output, Opt. Compressed trajectory (portable
                                   xdr format)
-cpi NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Input, Opt!  Checkpoint file
-cpo NVT_sam33_water8000.cpt  Output, Opt. Checkpoint file
  -c NVT_sam33_water8000.gro  Output       Structure file: gro g96 pdb etc.
  -e NVT_sam33_water8000.edr  Output       Energy file
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
  -g NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output       Log file
-dhdlNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-fieldVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tableVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tabletf_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-tablepT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-tablebT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Input, Opt.  xvgr/xmgr file
-rerunVT_sam33_water8000.xtc  Input, Opt.  Trajectory: xtc trr trj gro g96
                                   pdb cpt
-tpi NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-tpidNVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ei NVT_sam33_water8000.edi  Input, Opt.  ED sampling input
 -eo NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

  -j NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Input, Opt.  General coupling stuff
 -jo NVT_sam33_water8000.gct  Output, Opt. General coupling stuff
-ffoutVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-devoutT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
-runavVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -px NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -pf NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ro NVT_sam33_water8000.xvg  Output, Opt. xvgr/xmgr file
 -ra NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rs NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
 -rt NVT_sam33_water8000.log  Output, Opt. Log file
-mtx NVT_sam33_water8000.mtx  Output, Opt. Hessian matrix
 -dn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Output, Opt. Index file
-multidirsam33_water8000  Input, Opt., Mult. Run directory
-membedT_sam33_water8000.dat  Input, Opt.  Generic data file
 -mp NVT_sam33_water8000.top  Input, Opt.  Topology file
 -mn NVT_sam33_water8000.ndx  Input, Opt.  Index file

------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

Option       Type   Value   Description
------------------------------------------------------
-[no]h       bool   no      Print help info and quit
-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core

                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping

                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

                            file options

-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping

                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility

                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica

-[no]version bool   no      Print version info and quit
-nice        int    0       Set the nicelevel
-deffnm      string NVT_sam33_water8000  Set the default filename for all
                            file options
-xvg         enum   xmgrace  xvg plot formatting: xmgrace, xmgr or none
-[no]pd      bool   no      Use particle decompostion
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
-nsteps      step   -2      Run this number of steps, overrides .mdp file
                            option
-maxh        real   0.1     Terminate after 0.99 times this time (hours)
-multi       int    0       Do multiple simulations in parallel
-replex      int    0       Attempt replica exchange periodically with this
                            period (steps)
-nex         int    0       Number of random exchanges to carry out each
                            exchange interval (N^3 is one suggestion).  -nex
                            zero or not specified gives neighbor replica
                            exchange.
-reseed      int    -1      Seed for replica exchange, -1 is generate a seed
-[no]ionize  bool   no      Do a simulation including the effect of an X-Ray
                            bombardment on your system

-dd          vector 0 0 0   Domain decomposition grid, 0 is optimize
-ddorder     enum   interleave  DD node order: interleave, pp_pme or cartesian
-npme        int    -1      Number of separate nodes to be used for PME, -1
                            is guess
-nt          int    0       Total number of threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntmpi       int    0       Number of thread-MPI threads to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp       int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is guess)
-ntomp_pme   int    0       Number of OpenMP threads per MPI process/thread
                            to start (0 is -ntomp)
-pin         enum   auto    Fix threads (or processes) to specific cores:
                            auto, on or off
-pinoffset   int    0       The starting logical core number for pinning to
                            cores; used to avoid pinning threads from
                            different mdrun instances to the same core
-pinstride   int    0       Pinning distance in logical cores for threads,
                            use 0 to minimize the number of threads per
                            physical core
-gpu_id      string         List of GPU device id-s to use, specifies the
                            per-node PP rank to GPU mapping
-[no]ddcheck bool   yes     Check for all bonded interactions with DD
-rdd         real   0       The maximum distance for bonded interactions with
                            DD (nm), 0 is determine from initial coordinates
-rcon        real   0       Maximum distance for P-LINCS (nm), 0 is estimate
-dlb         enum   auto    Dynamic load balancing (with DD): auto, no or yes
-dds         real   0.8     Minimum allowed dlb scaling of the DD cell size
-gcom        int    -1      Global communication frequency
-nb          enum   auto    Calculate non-bonded interactions on: auto, cpu,
                            gpu or gpu_cpu
-[no]tunepme bool   yes     Optimize PME load between PP/PME nodes or GPU/CPU
-[no]testverlet bool   yes     Test the Verlet non-bonded scheme
-[no]v       bool   yes     Be loud and noisy
-[no]compact bool   yes     Write a compact log file
-[no]seppot  bool   no      Write separate V and dVdl terms for each
                            interaction type and node to the log file(s)
-pforce      real   -1      Print all forces larger than this (kJ/mol nm)
-[no]reprod  bool   no      Try to avoid optimizations that affect binary
                            reproducibility
-cpt         real   15      Checkpoint interval (minutes)
-[no]cpnum   bool   no      Keep and number checkpoint files
-[no]append  bool   yes     Append to previous output files when continuing
                            from checkpoint instead of adding the simulation
                            part number to all file names
